================



 Posted in **MTGO Standings**
 on May 2, 2022

* [Decklists](#decklists)
* [Standings](#standings)

Bracket
-------

**(4) Boin, 2-1**






 (5) Gn42

### Finals






**(1) Hamuda, 2-0**
